vendor/abiword-2.4.5/abipbx/AbiWord-DMG-ReadMe/InvisibleAnt/Templates.html:62:      <p>If you scroll down through the list, you will see a lot of templates called &quot;normal.awt&quot;, &quot;normal.awt-en_CA&quot;, &quot;normal.awt-en_GB&quot;, &quot;normal.awt-ca_ES&quot;, and so on. The &quot;-en&quot;, &quot;-ca&quot;, etc., indicate language, and the &quot;_CA&quot;, &quot;_GB&quot;, etc., indicate country. Choose one which suits your preferred default language for spell checking. Some of these have different default page sizes also - for example, &quot;normal.awt-en_GB&quot; is set to page size A4.</p>
